style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Each of these measures excludes from the most directly comparable GAAP measures the impact of certain items.&#160; Management believes these adjusted measures are useful to investors because they assist an investor&#8217;s understanding of the impact of these items on the comparability of the Company&#8217;s operations from year-to-year.&#160; Excluding the impact of these items also enables investors to compare our underlying operational results and trends before other charges and income items that are considered by management as not related to the Company&#8217;s core operations.&#160; Management uses these adjusted measures to monitor and evaluate operating performance and also for internal planning purposes.&#160; These measures are subject to certain limitations because they do not reflect all charges, income, or other items that were actually recognized by the Company in accordance with GAAP.&#160; As a result, investors should consider these non-GAAP measures in addition to, and not as a substitute for, or superior to, financial performance measures presented in accordance with GAAP.&#160; In addition, these adjusted measures may not be calculated in the same manner as adjusted measures presented by other companies.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">During the third quarter, the Company entered into an agreement to sell its Pressure Sensitive Materials business segment. The results of this segment are reported as discontinued operations.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Neenah, Wisconsin, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">October&#160;23, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;- Bemis Company, Inc. (NYSE:BMS) today reported </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;diluted earnings per share from continuing operations of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.61</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.47</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per share for the same quarter of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Excluding the items detailed in the attached schedule, &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Earnings per Share,&#8221; adjusted diluted earnings per share from continuing operations for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of 2013 would have been </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.55</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Our record third quarter results reflect continued progress in the implementation of our long-term strategy,&#8221; said William Austen, Bemis Company&#8217;s President and Chief Executive Officer. &#8220;Our Global Packaging business delivered solid operating profit improvement, driven by our strong pricing discipline and unit volume growth in our high margin target end markets around the world.  In our U.S. Packaging business, operating margins increased and we continued to commercialize new business awards.  As we move forward, we are focused on further improving performance metrics through continued pricing discipline, capacity investments, and operational improvements that will deliver more efficient scale-up of our growth projects.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sA0C204C7BEEBE2CE6BFCA17E68471D2C"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">BUSINESS SEGMENT RESULTS </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">U.S. Packaging</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">U.S. Packaging net sales of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$716.7 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;represented a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">4.5 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the same period of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  The first quarter 2014 divestiture of the Paper Packaging Division reduced sales by </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">5.6 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Excluding the impact of divestitures, the 1.1 percent increase in net sales reflects the benefit of increased selling prices and improved sales mix</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">U.S. Packaging operating profit for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">95.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">13.3 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">$81.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">10.9 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, in the same period of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Excluding facility consolidation costs in 2013, segment adjusted operating profit would have been </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">$97.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">13.0 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales. (See attached schedule: &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Operating Profit.&#8221;)  Operating profit results reflect the benefit of sales mix improvements and the adverse impact of costs and manufacturing inefficiencies related to the commercialization of new business.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:6px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Global Packaging</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:16px;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Global Packaging net sales for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">$381.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;represented an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">2.9 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared to the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Currency translation decreased net sales by </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2.5 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Excluding the impact of currency translation, Global Packaging net sales increased 5.4 percent from the prior year, reflecting unit volume growth in addition to favorable sales price and mix. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Global Packaging operating profit for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">$32.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">8.6 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">$28.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">7.6 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, for the same period in </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  The net effect of currency translation decreased operating profit during the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of 2014 by $1.0 million.  Margin improvement in this segment reflects the favorable impact of increased sales of value added packaging for medical device, pharmaceutical, and perishable food applications.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">DISCONTINUED OPERATIONS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">On September 8, 2014, the Company entered into an agreement to sell its Pressure Sensitive Materials business segment. Management expects the transaction to close during the fourth quarter of 2014.  Considering the agreed upon price, management recorded a non-cash impairment charge to goodwill.  The results of this segment and the impairment charge related to the transaction are reported as discontinued operations.</font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">CAPITAL STRUCTURE AND CASH FLOW</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Total company net debt to adjusted EBITDA was 2.1 times at September&#160;30, 2014, slightly above our target ratio of 2.0 times.  Net debt is defined as total debt less cash, and adjusted EBITDA is defined as last twelve months adjusted total company operating income plus depreciation and amortization.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Cash flow from operations for the quarter of $121.1 million compared to $160.0 million for third quarter of 2013, reflecting generally higher levels of working capital associated with higher raw material costs, increased inventory levels, and higher selling prices.  These working capital increases support new product commercialization and strong customer demand for value-added products.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sA0C204C7BEEBE2CE6BFCA17E68471D2C"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">On August 1, 2014, public notes totaling $400 million matured.  Management refinanced these notes with lower interest rate debt, comprised of a $200 million bank term loan that matures in 2022 and $200 million of commercial paper.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">2014 OUTLOOK </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">In anticipation of the sale of the Pressure Sensitive Materials business segment, management established new guidance for continuing operations.  Management expects adjusted diluted earnings per share from continuing operations to be in the range of $0.53 to $0.58 for the fourth quarter and in the range of $2.26 to $2.31 for the full year 2014.  Considering the results of discontinued operations, management&#8217;s new full year guidance range is consistent with the middle of its previously stated full year guidance range.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Management revised the guidance for total year 2014 cash from operations to reflect inflation, the timing of the Pressure Sensitive Materials divestiture, and generally higher levels of working capital expected to support new product commercialization and strong customer demand for value-added products.  Full year 2014 cash flow from operating activities is expected to be in the range of $375 million to $400 million.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Management continues to expect the effective income tax rate for the full year 2014 to be approximately 34.5 percent and total year 2014 capital expenditures to be approximately $175 million.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">PRESENTATION OF NON-GAAP INFORMATION</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This press release refers to non-GAAP financial measures: adjusted operating profit, adjusted operating profit as a percentage of net sales, net debt to adjusted EBITDA, and adjusted diluted earnings per share.  These non-GAAP financial measures adjust for factors that are unusual or unpredictable.  These measures exclude the impact of certain amounts related to facility consolidation and plant closure activities including employee-related costs, equipment relocation costs, lease termination payments, accelerated depreciation, and the write-down of equipment.  These measures also exclude gains or losses on sales of property and divestitures and certain acquisition-related expenses including transaction expenses, due diligence expenses, professional and legal fees, purchase accounting adjustments for inventory and order backlog, integration expenses, the cash portion of any acquisition earn-out payments recorded as compensation expenses, and changes in fair value of deferred acquisition payments.  This adjusted information should not be construed as an alternative to results determined in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America (GAAP).  It is provided solely to assist in an investor's understanding of the impact of these items on the comparability of the Company's ongoing business operations.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">3</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sA0C204C7BEEBE2CE6BFCA17E68471D2C"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Statements in this release that are not historical, including statements relating to the expected future performance of the Company, are considered &#8220;forward-looking&#8221; and are presented pursuant to the safe harbor provisions of the Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.  Such content is subject to certain risks and uncertainties, including but not limited to general economic conditions, future changes in cost or availability of raw materials, our ability to adjust selling prices, consumer buying patterns, changes in customer order patterns, the results of competitive bid processes, costs associated with the pursuit of business combinations or divestitures, plant closures, a failure in our information technology infrastructure or applications, foreign currency fluctuations, unexpected costs associated with production relocation, changes in working capital requirements, changes in government regulations, and the availability and related cost of financing from banks and capital markets.  Actual future results and trends may differ materially from historical results or those projected in any such forward-looking statements depending on a variety of factors which are detailed in the Company's regular SEC filings including the most recently filed Form 10-K for the year ended December&#160;31, 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">INVESTOR CONFERENCE CALL</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Bemis Company, Inc. will webcast an investor telephone conference regarding its third quarter 2014 financial results this morning at 11 a.m., Eastern Time.  Individuals may listen to the call on the Internet at www.bemis.com under &#8220;Investor Relations.&#8221;  Listeners are urged to check the website ahead of time to ensure their computers are configured for the audio stream.  Instructions for obtaining the required, free, downloadable software are available in a pre-event system test on the site.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">ABOUT BEMIS COMPANY, INC.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Bemis Company, Inc. is a major supplier of packaging and pressure sensitive materials used by leading food, consumer products, healthcare, and other companies worldwide.  Founded in 1858, Bemis Company is included in the S&amp;P 500 index of stocks and reported 2013 net sales of $4.5 billion from continuing operations.  Bemis has a strong technical base in polymer chemistry, film extrusion, coating and laminating, printing, and converting.  Headquartered in Neenah, Wisconsin, Bemis employs approximately 19,000 individuals worldwide.  More information about Bemis is available at our website, www.bemis.com.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:6px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">For additional information please contact:</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Erin M.
